  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0643562f-b1a5-4179-b9dd-72822d2a29ee'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer13517334848996075156">Miss Massie Block and her in-famous come backs. Thats what you take out of this series, you'd find them literally every 3 pages, they're everywhere! <br/><br/>i.e. "Kristen, why don't you send me a postcard from Morocco?" "It sounds like your swimming in de-Nile."<br/><br/>Effortless yet so cunning, Massie Block's comebacks are symbolical of all The Clique series is, quite literally a joke that you laugh about maybe, once, and then move on to something better.<br/><br/>Recommend: As I read this when in middle school, it serv</span>
  <span id="freeText13517334848996075156" style="display:none">Miss Massie Block and her in-famous come backs. Thats what you take out of this series, you'd find them literally every 3 pages, they're everywhere! <br /><br />i.e. "Kristen, why don't you send me a postcard from Morocco?" "It sounds like your swimming in de-Nile."<br /><br />Effortless yet so cunning, Massie Block's comebacks are symbolical of all The Clique series is, quite literally a joke that you laugh about maybe, once, and then move on to something better.<br /><br />Recommend: As I read this when in middle school, it served its purpose, a middle school read, that maturing girls get hooked onto, evidence in how many of these endless books there are! And I thought the Summer Series was going to be a stretch for Lisi, I guess not, she's still got more Massie-backs in there! </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dJpQ/hl+m7wQGFNYDZedNNvGIxu+u64lV+YGKaGmNdGTJ8U6ULo9n96kydjcseT8LljPR3o93sUZKa8IAwxk7Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MkcYkYHgujgbfGGBGHJotpDfi7dozFM4c2OrdJsiCl3V+o1VyCQcG9XA+wHJVBF+ZUFn66xKI9g9rAJVOYhbYQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7093078210236111366"><i>Lisi Harrison</i> is the author of the #1 New York Times best-selling series "The Clique", "Alphas", "Monster High," Pretenders," and her first adult novel: "The Dirty Book Club" out 10.10.17. Lisi was born in Toronto, Canada, and lived in NYC for 15 years while she worked at MTV. She now lives in Laguna Beach, CA and is a member or her own Dirty Book Club. <br/><br/><br/><br/></span>
